Alright, bro. Here are the question sets for the first four Biology chapters, based on the KCET previous years' questions pattern.

***

&& The Living World

#### Easy

**1.** The process by which living organisms produce offspring of their own kind is called:
A. Growth
B. Metabolism
C. Reproduction
D. Consciousness
**Correct Answer: C**

**2.** Which of the following is considered a defining property of living organisms?
A. Growth
B. Reproduction
C. Consciousness (Response to stimuli)
D. Increase in mass
**Correct Answer: C**

**3.** The system of providing a scientific name with two components to a living organism is called:
A. Taxonomy
B. Classification
C. Binomial nomenclature
D. Systematics
**Correct Answer: C**

**4.** Who is known as the father of taxonomy?
A. Charles Darwin
B. Gregor Mendel
C. Carolus Linnaeus
D. Aristotle
**Correct Answer: C**

**5.** In the scientific name *Mangifera indica*, the name 'indica' represents the:
A. Genus
B. Species
C. Family
D. Order
**Correct Answer: B**

**6.** The correct hierarchical order of taxonomic categories is:
A. Kingdom, Phylum, Class, Order, Family, Genus, Species
B. Kingdom, Phylum, Order, Class, Family, Genus, Species
C. Kingdom, Class, Phylum, Family, Order, Genus, Species
D. Phylum, Kingdom, Class, Order, Family, Genus, Species
**Correct Answer: A**

**7.** A herbarium is a storehouse of:
A. Living plant specimens
B. Dried and pressed plant specimens
C. Living animal specimens
D. Preserved animal specimens
**Correct Answer: B**

**8.** The scientific name for human beings is:
A. *Canis familiaris*
B. *Felis catus*
C. *Mangifera indica*
D. *Homo sapiens*
**Correct Answer: D**

**9.** Which of the following is a taxonomical aid?
A. Museum
B. Botanical Garden
C. Herbarium
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**10.** The basic unit of classification is the:
A. Genus
B. Family
C. Species
D. Kingdom
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** Systematics is the study of:
A. Naming organisms
B. Classifying organisms
C. The diversity of organisms and their evolutionary relationships
D. The structure of organisms
**Correct Answer: C**

**12.** The book 'Systema Naturae' was written by:
A. Darwin
B. Lamarck
C. Linnaeus
D. Whittaker
**Correct Answer: C**

**13.** A group of related species is called a:
A. Family
B. Order
C. Class
D. Genus
**Correct Answer: D**

**14.** In binomial nomenclature, the scientific name is printed in:
A. Bold
B. Underlined
C. Italics
D. All capitals
**Correct Answer: C**

**15.** The sum total of all the chemical reactions occurring in our body is called:
A. Anabolism
B. Catabolism
C. Metabolism
D. Homeostasis
**Correct Answer: C**

**16.** A key is a taxonomical aid used for the identification of plants and animals based on:
A. Similarities only
B. Dissimilarities only
C. Both similarities and dissimilarities
D. Evolutionary relationships
**Correct Answer: C**

**17.** The main purpose of a botanical garden is:
A. To provide a beautiful landscape
B. To serve as a collection of living plants for reference (ex-situ conservation)
C. To preserve plant specimens on sheets
D. To study the local flora only
**Correct Answer: B**

**18.** The family of humans (*Homo sapiens*) is:
A. Hominidae
B. Primata
C. Mammalia
D. Chordata
**Correct Answer: A**

**19.** Which of the following represents an order?
A. Solanum
B. Poaceae
C. Polymoniales
D. Dicotyledonae
**Correct Answer: C**

**20.** Growth in living organisms is characterized by an increase in:
A. Mass only
B. Number of individuals only
C. Both mass and number of individuals
D. Size only
**Correct Answer: C**

---

#### Medium

**21.** As we go from species to kingdom in a taxonomic hierarchy, the number of common characteristics:
A. Will increase
B. Will decrease
C. Remains the same
D. May increase or decrease
**Correct Answer: B**

**22.** Which of the following 'suffixes' used for units of classification in plants indicates a taxonomic category of 'family'?
A. -ales
B. -onae
C. -aceae
D. -ae
**Correct Answer: C**

**23.** The label of a herbarium sheet does not carry information on:
A. Date of collection
B. Name of collector
C. Local names
D. Height of the plant
**Correct Answer: D**

**24.** Which of the following is against the rules of ICBN (International Code for Botanical Nomenclature)?
A. Scientific names are in Latin and printed in italics.
B. The first word in a biological name represents the genus.
C. Both words in a biological name, when handwritten, are underlined separately.
D. The names of the authors appear after the species name and are written in italics.
**Correct Answer: D**

**25.** A taxonomical key is based on a pair of contrasting characters known as a:
A. Taxon
B. Couplet
C. Lead
D. Monograph
**Correct Answer: B**

**26.** The scientific names of the leopard, tiger, and lion are *Panthera pardus*, *Panthera tigris*, and *Panthera leo* respectively. They all belong to the same:
A. Species
B. Genus
C. Family
D. Order
**Correct Answer: B**

**27.** Which of the following is not a correct hierarchical order?
A. Class, Order, Family
B. Phylum, Order, Class
C. Kingdom, Phylum, Class
D. Family, Genus, Species
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** The term 'Systematics' refers to:
A. Identification and classification of plants and animals
B. Nomenclature and identification of plants and animals
C. Diversity of kinds of organisms and their relationship
D. Different kinds of organisms and their classification
**Correct Answer: C**

**29.** The 'twin characteristics' of growth are:
A. Increase in mass and differentiation
B. Increase in mass and increase in number of individuals
C. Increase in size and reproduction
D. Increase in number and complexity
**Correct Answer: B**

**30.** A monograph contains information on:
A. All species found in a particular area
B. One specific family or genus
C. Any one taxon
D. All the plants of a region
**Correct Answer: C**

**31.** The practical purpose of classification of living organisms is to:
A. Explain the origin of living organisms
B. Trace the evolution of living organisms
C. Name the living organisms
D. Facilitate identification of unknown organisms
**Correct Answer: D**

**32.** In mule, the growth and metabolism are present but it cannot reproduce. This shows that:
A. Reproduction is not a characteristic of living things
B. Reproduction is not a defining feature of living things
C. Mules are not living
D. All living things do not grow
**Correct Answer: B**

**33.** Which of the following combinations is correct for wheat?
A. Genus *Triticum*, family Poaceae, order Poales, class Monocotyledonae
B. Genus *Triticum*, family Poaceae, order Sapindales, class Dicotyledonae
C. Genus *Triticum*, family Anacardiaceae, order Poales, class Monocotyledonae
D. Genus *Triticum*, family Poaceae, order Poales, class Dicotyledonae
**Correct Answer: A**

**34.** Which taxonomical aid provides information for the identification of names of species found in an area?
A. Monograph
B. Manual
C. Flora
D. Key
**Correct Answer: B**

**35.** The scientific term for biological classification categories is the:
A. Taxon
B. Phylum
C. Species
D. Domain
**Correct Answer: A**

**36.** A group of individuals which are able to breed among themselves and produce their own kind is known as a:
A. Genus
B. Species
C. Family
D. Order
**Correct Answer: B**

**37.** The Royal Botanical Garden is located in:
A. Kew, England
B. Lucknow, India
C. Howrah, India
D. Berlin, Germany
**Correct Answer: A**

**38.** The family 'Solanaceae' and 'Convolvulaceae' are included in the order:
A. Poales
B. Sapindales
C. Polymoniales
D. Rosales
**Correct Answer: C**

**39.** The largest collections of plant and animal specimens are found in:
A. Botanical gardens and Herbaria
B. Museums and Zoological parks
C. Herbaria and Museums
D. Botanical gardens and Zoological parks
**Correct Answer: B**

**40.** A zoological park is a place where:
A. Wild animals are kept in protected environments under human care
B. Preserved animal specimens are kept for study
C. Plant specimens are preserved
D. Living plants are grown for identification
**Correct Answer: A**

---

#### Hard

**41.** Choose the correct statement from the following:
A. In unicellular organisms, growth and reproduction are mutually exclusive events.
B. The scientific name of a species is a binomial having two specific names.
C. Growth in living organisms is from inside.
D. Metabolic reactions can be demonstrated in-vitro, hence they are a defining feature of life.
**Correct Answer: C**

**42.** The taxonomic keys are based on contrasting characters generally in a pair called a couplet. Each statement in the key is called a:
A. Taxon
B. Lead
C. Category
D. Rank
**Correct Answer: B**

**43.** Which of the following statements about the species concept is incorrect?
A. A species is a group of morphologically similar individuals.
B. Members of a species can interbreed to produce fertile offspring.
C. The concept of species is a dynamic concept that changes with evolution.
D. A species is the largest unit of classification.
**Correct Answer: D**

**44.** If an organism is in the same class but not in the same family, then it must also be in the same:
A. Genus
B. Species
C. Order
D. Phylum
**Correct Answer: D**

**45.** A student identifies an object to be a living thing. Which of the following characteristics is the most definitive reason?
A. The object is growing in size.
B. The object is showing movement.
C. The object is showing metabolic processes.
D. The object has a definite shape.
**Correct Answer: C**

**46.** The number of obligate categories in the taxonomic hierarchy is:
A. 5
B. 7
C. 9
D. 11
**Correct Answer: B**

**47.** Consider the following statements: (i) Genus comprises a group of related species. (ii) A taxon represents a taxonomic group of any ranking. (iii) Family comprises a group of related orders. (iv) Taxonomic key is a tool for identification. Which of the statements are correct?
A. (i), (ii), and (iv)
B. (i), (iii), and (iv)
C. (i), (ii), and (iii)
D. (ii), (iii), and (iv)
**Correct Answer: A**

**48.** The correct representation of the scientific name for mango is:
A. Mangifera Indica
B. *mangifera indica*
C. *Mangifera indica*
D. Mangifera indica
**Correct Answer: C**

**49.** Which one of the taxonomical aids can give a comprehensive account of complete compiled information of any one genus or family at a particular time?
A. Flora
B. Key
C. Monograph
D. Herbarium
**Correct Answer: C**

**50.** The 'Biological species concept' emphasizes:
A. Morphological similarity
B. Geographic isolation
C. Reproductive isolation
D. Ecological niche
**Correct Answer: C**

***

&& Biological Classification

#### Easy

**1.** The Five Kingdom Classification was proposed by:
A. Carolus Linnaeus
B. R.H. Whittaker
C. Aristotle
D. Ernst Haeckel
**Correct Answer: B**

**2.** The kingdom that includes prokaryotic organisms is:
A. Protista
B. Fungi
C. Monera
D. Plantae
**Correct Answer: C**

**3.** Bacteria with a spherical shape are called:
A. Bacilli
B. Cocci
C. Spirilla
D. Vibrio
**Correct Answer: B**

**4.** Which of the following is not a kingdom in Whittaker's classification?
A. Fungi
B. Animalia
C. Protista
D. Viruses
**Correct Answer: D**

**5.** The kingdom Protista includes:
A. Unicellular prokaryotes
B. Unicellular eukaryotes
C. Multicellular prokaryotes
D. Multicellular eukaryotes
**Correct Answer: B**

**6.** The cell walls of fungi are made of:
A. Cellulose
B. Pectin
C. Chitin
D. Peptidoglycan
**Correct Answer: C**

**7.** Viruses are considered non-living because they:
A. Are very small
B. Lack a cellular structure and cannot reproduce on their own
C. Cause diseases
D. Are found everywhere
**Correct Answer: B**

**8.** The protein coat of a virus is called the:
A. Capsomere
B. Capsid
C. Nucleoid
D. Virion
**Correct Answer: B**

**9.** Lichens are a symbiotic association between:
A. Fungi and bacteria
B. Algae and bacteria
C. Fungi and roots of higher plants
D. Algae and fungi
**Correct Answer: D**

**10.** Which group of organisms is known as the 'imperfect fungi'?
A. Phycomycetes
B. Ascomycetes
C. Basidiomycetes
D. Deuteromycetes
**Correct Answer: D**

**11.** Diatoms, the chief producers in the oceans, belong to the kingdom:
A. Monera
B. Protista
C. Fungi
D. Plantae
**Correct Answer: B**

**12.** Archaebacteria that live in salty areas are called:
A. Methanogens
B. Halophiles
C. Thermoacidophiles
D. Cyanobacteria
**Correct Answer: B**

**13.** The mode of nutrition in the kingdom Fungi is primarily:
A. Autotrophic
B. Photosynthetic
C. Saprophytic or parasitic
D. Holozoic
**Correct Answer: C**

**14.** The main criteria for the five kingdom classification did NOT include:
A. Cell structure
B. Mode of nutrition
C. Phylogenetic relationships
D. Mode of reproduction
**Correct Answer: D**
*(Note: While reproduction is a character, the other three were the primary criteria.)*

**15.** Viroids are infectious agents that consist of:
A. A protein coat only
B. A nucleic acid core only
C. Free, low molecular weight RNA
D. Free, low molecular weight DNA
**Correct Answer: C**

**16.** Red tides in the sea are caused by the rapid multiplication of:
A. Diatoms
B. Euglenoids
C. Dinoflagellates
D. Slime moulds
**Correct Answer: C**

**17.** The network of thread-like structures that forms the body of a fungus is called:
A. Hyphae
B. Mycelium
C. Spores
D. Rhizoids
**Correct Answer: B**

**18.** The bacterial cell wall is composed of:
A. Chitin
B. Cellulose
C. Peptidoglycan
D. Lignin
**Correct Answer: C**

**19.** Mycorrhiza is a symbiotic association between:
A. Algae and fungi
B. Fungi and bacteria
C. Fungi and roots of higher plants
D. Algae and roots of higher plants
**Correct Answer: C**

**20.** Yeast belongs to which class of fungi?
A. Phycomycetes
B. Ascomycetes
C. Basidiomycetes
D. Deuteromycetes
**Correct Answer: B**

---

#### Medium

**21.** Which of the following statements about viruses is correct?
A. They have their own metabolic system.
B. They contain both DNA and RNA.
C. They are obligate intracellular parasites.
D. They can be killed by antibiotics.
**Correct Answer: C**

**22.** The cell wall of diatoms is indestructible due to the presence of:
A. Chitin
B. Silica
C. Calcium carbonate
D. Peptidoglycan
**Correct Answer: B**

**23.** In the five kingdom classification, Chlamydomonas and Chlorella have been included in:
A. Plantae
B. Algae
C. Protista
D. Monera
**Correct Answer: C**

**24.** Which of the following groups of fungi are commonly known as sac-fungi?
A. Phycomycetes
B. Deuteromycetes
C. Basidiomycetes
D. Ascomycetes
**Correct Answer: D**

**25.** The dikaryotic phase (n+n) is a characteristic feature of which fungal classes?
A. Phycomycetes and Ascomycetes
B. Ascomycetes and Basidiomycetes
C. Phycomycetes and Deuteromycetes
D. Basidiomycetes and Deuteromycetes
**Correct Answer: B**

**26.** Which of the following organisms completely lacks a cell wall?
A. Cyanobacteria
B. Saccharomyces (Yeast)
C. Mycoplasma
D. Diatoms
**Correct Answer: C**

**27.** The asexual spores produced endogenously in Phycomycetes are called:
A. Conidia
B. Zoospores or Aplanospores
C. Oospores
D. Ascospores
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** The function of the algal partner in a lichen is to:
A. Provide protection
B. Absorb water and minerals
C. Prepare food
D. Provide a structure for reproduction
**Correct Answer: C**

**29.** The disease 'mad cow disease' in cattle is caused by an abnormally folded protein called a:
A. Virus
B. Viroid
C. Prion
D. Bacterium
**Correct Answer: C**

**30.** The main difference between Gram-positive and Gram-negative bacteria lies in the composition of their:
A. Cell membrane
B. Cytoplasm
C. Flagella
D. Cell wall
**Correct Answer: D**

**31.** Slime moulds are characterized by the formation of an aggregate called:
A. Mycelium
B. Plasmodium
C. Protonema
D. Fruiting body
**Correct Answer: B**

**32.** Which of the following is incorrect about Euglenoids?
A. They have a protein-rich layer called a pellicle.
B. They are photosynthetic in the presence of sunlight.
C. They are always heterotrophic.
D. They have two flagella, a short and a long one.
**Correct Answer: C**

**33.** Which of the following statements is incorrect?
A. Yeasts are unicellular fungi.
B. The vegetative body of a fungus is called mycelium.
C. Deuteromycetes reproduce only by asexual spores.
D. Asexual reproduction in fungi occurs only through conidia.
**Correct Answer: D**

**34.** Which of the following is not a member of kingdom Protista?
A. Amoeba
B. Paramecium
C. Euglena
D. Aspergillus
**Correct Answer: D**

**35.** The main basis of classification in the kingdom Fungi is:
A. Mycelium structure
B. Mode of spore formation
C. Fruiting bodies
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**36.** Methanogens, a type of archaebacteria, are responsible for the production of:
A. Methane in marshy areas
B. Biogas from the gut of ruminants
C. Methane in paddy fields
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**37.** The five-kingdom system of classification is not applicable to:
A. Algae
B. Fungi
C. Viruses
D. Bacteria
**Correct Answer: C**

**38.** In which class of fungi are sexual spores produced exogenously on a structure called the basidium?
A. Phycomycetes
B. Ascomycetes
C. Basidiomycetes
D. Deuteromycetes
**Correct Answer: C**

**39.** The pigment responsible for the red color in red algae and some cyanobacteria is:
A. Chlorophyll a
B. Fucoxanthin
C. Phycoerythrin
D. Chlorophyll b
**Correct Answer: C**

**40.** A heterocyst in cyanobacteria is a specialized cell that performs:
A. Photosynthesis
B. Nitrogen fixation
C. Reproduction
D. Storage
**Correct Answer: B**

---

#### Hard

**41.** Select the wrong statement:
A. The walls of diatoms are easily destructible.
B. 'Diatomaceous earth' is formed by the cell walls of diatoms.
C. Diatoms are chief producers in the oceans.
D. Diatoms are microscopic and float passively in water.
**Correct Answer: A**

**42.** Which of the following statements is incorrect for viroids?
A. They cause potato spindle tuber disease.
B. They are smaller than viruses.
C. Their RNA is of high molecular weight.
D. They lack a protein coat.
**Correct Answer: C**

**43.** The sexual cycle in fungi involves three steps in the correct sequence:
A. Karyogamy, Plasmogamy, Meiosis
B. Plasmogamy, Karyogamy, Meiosis
C. Meiosis, Plasmogamy, Karyogamy
D. Plasmogamy, Meiosis, Karyogamy
**Correct Answer: B**

**44.** Pick up the wrong statement:
A. Some fungi are edible.
B. Nuclear membrane is present in Monera.
C. Cell wall is absent in Animalia.
D. Protists have photosynthetic and heterotrophic modes of nutrition.
**Correct Answer: B**

**45.** Which of the following is true for the kingdom Animalia?
A. They are multicellular, eukaryotic, and autotrophic.
B. They are unicellular, prokaryotic, and heterotrophic.
C. They are multicellular, eukaryotic, and heterotrophic with a cell wall.
D. They are multicellular, eukaryotic, and heterotrophic without a cell wall.
**Correct Answer: D**

**46.** The difference between a virus and a viroid is:
A. Absence of protein coat in viroid but present in virus.
B. Presence of low molecular weight RNA in virus but absent in viroid.
C. Both A and B
D. None of the above
**Correct Answer: A**

**47.** In the context of the two-kingdom classification, which of the following was a major drawback?
A. It did not distinguish between eukaryotes and prokaryotes.
B. It did not distinguish between unicellular and multicellular organisms.
C. It did not distinguish between photosynthetic and non-photosynthetic organisms.
D. All of the above.
**Correct Answer: D**

**48.** A coenocytic mycelium is:
A. Aseptate and multinucleate
B. Septate and uninucleate
C. Aseptate and uninucleate
D. Septate and multinucleate
**Correct Answer: A**

**49.** Which of the following is not a characteristic of protozoan protists?
A. They are believed to be primitive relatives of animals.
B. All protozoans have flagella for locomotion.
C. They are heterotrophs and live as predators or parasites.
D. *Trypanosoma* is a protozoan that causes sleeping sickness.
**Correct Answer: B**

**50.** The genetic material of a bacteriophage is typically:
A. Single-stranded RNA
B. Double-stranded RNA
C. Single-stranded DNA
D. Double-stranded DNA
**Correct Answer: D**

***

&& Plant Kingdom

#### Easy

**1.** The dominant phase in the life cycle of a bryophyte is the:
A. Sporophyte
B. Gametophyte
C. Zygote
D. Spore
**Correct Answer: B**

**2.** In which group of plants is the plant body not differentiated into root, stem, and leaves?
A. Algae
B. Bryophytes
C. Pteridophytes
D. Gymnosperms
**Correct Answer: A**

**3.** Double fertilization is a characteristic feature of:
A. Algae
B. Fungi
C. Gymnosperms
D. Angiosperms
**Correct Answer: D**

**4.** The main plant body of a pteridophyte is a:
A. Gametophyte which is dependent on the sporophyte
B. Sporophyte which is dependent on the gametophyte
C. Sporophyte which is independent
D. Gametophyte which is independent
**Correct Answer: C**

**5.** The female sex organ in bryophytes and pteridophytes is called the:
A. Antheridium
B. Oogonium
C. Archegonium
D. Carpel
**Correct Answer: C**

**6.** Which of the following is an example of a green alga?
A. *Sargassum*
B. *Fucus*
C. *Chlamydomonas*
D. *Polysiphonia*
**Correct Answer: C**

**7.** Plants that possess vascular tissues (xylem and phloem) but lack seeds are:
A. Algae
B. Bryophytes
C. Pteridophytes
D. Gymnosperms
**Correct Answer: C**

**8.** The ovules in gymnosperms are:
A. Enclosed within an ovary
B. Exposed (naked)
C. Absent
D. Fused together
**Correct Answer: B**

**9.** The life cycle pattern in which the diploid sporophyte is the dominant phase is called:
A. Haplontic
B. Diplontic
C. Haplo-diplontic
D. Mono-phasic
**Correct Answer: B**

**10.** Agar, a commercial product, is obtained from:
A. Green algae
B. Brown algae
C. Red algae
D. Blue-green algae
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** The first terrestrial plants to possess vascular tissues are:
A. Bryophytes
B. Pteridophytes
C. Gymnosperms
D. Angiosperms
**Correct Answer: B**

**12.** The fusion of two gametes dissimilar in size is termed:
A. Isogamy
B. Anisogamy
C. Oogamy
D. Zoogamy
**Correct Answer: B**

**13.** The dominant photosynthetic pigment in brown algae (Phaeophyceae) is:
A. Chlorophyll a
B. Phycoerythrin
C. Fucoxanthin
D. Chlorophyll b
**Correct Answer: C**

**14.** In mosses, the spore germinates to form a filamentous structure called the:
A. Prothallus
B. Protonema
C. Thallus
D. Capsule
**Correct Answer: B**

**15.** The tallest tree species in the world, the redwood tree (*Sequoia*), is a:
A. Angiosperm
B. Gymnosperm
C. Pteridophyte
D. Bryophyte
**Correct Answer: B**

**16.** The stored food material in red algae (Rhodophyceae) is:
A. Starch
B. Mannitol and Laminarin
C. Glycogen
D. Floridean starch
**Correct Answer: D**

**17.** The production of two kinds of spores, microspores and megaspores, is known as:
A. Homospory
B. Heterospory
C. Isogamy
D. Anisogamy
**Correct Answer: B**

**18.** The main function of rhizoids in bryophytes is:
A. Photosynthesis
B. Conduction of water
C. Anchorage
D. Spore formation
**Correct Answer: C**

**19.** The endosperm in angiosperms is formed after fertilization and is typically:
A. Haploid (n)
B. Diploid (2n)
C. Triploid (3n)
D. Tetraploid (4n)
**Correct Answer: C**

**20.** Bryophytes are often called the 'amphibians of the plant kingdom' because they:
A. Live in water only
B. Live on land only
C. Require water for sexual reproduction
D. Can live in both hot and cold climates
**Correct Answer: C**

---

#### Medium

**21.** Select the correct statement:
A. The leaves of gymnosperms are not well adapted to extremes of climate.
B. In gymnosperms, the male and female gametophytes have an independent existence.
C. The sporophyte in liverworts is more elaborate than that in mosses.
D. *Salvinia* is a heterosporous pteridophyte.
**Correct Answer: D**

**22.** Which of the following is a correct match of an alga and its characteristic feature?
A. *Volvox* - Colonial, non-flagellated
B. *Chlamydomonas* - Unicellular, flagellated
C. *Spirogyra* - Filamentous, motile gametes
D. *Laminaria* - Unicellular, red alga
**Correct Answer: B**

**23.** The endosperm in gymnosperms is a:
A. Pre-fertilization tissue and is haploid (n)
B. Post-fertilization tissue and is triploid (3n)
C. Pre-fertilization tissue and is diploid (2n)
D. Post-fertilization tissue and is diploid (2n)
**Correct Answer: A**

**24.** The prothallus of a pteridophyte is a:
A. Small, multicellular, free-living, photosynthetic gametophyte
B. Large, unicellular, dependent, non-photosynthetic sporophyte
C. Small, unicellular, free-living, photosynthetic sporophyte
D. Large, multicellular, dependent, non-photosynthetic gametophyte
**Correct Answer: A**

**25.** The evolution of the seed habit is linked to:
A. The development of a dominant sporophyte
B. The development of heterospory
C. The requirement of water for fertilization
D. The absence of vascular tissue
**Correct Answer: B**

**26.** In the life cycle of a moss, the sporophyte:
A. Produces gametes that give rise to the gametophyte
B. Arises from a spore produced from the gametophyte
C. Is partially dependent on the gametophyte
D. Is the dominant and independent phase
**Correct Answer: C**

**27.** Which of the following is not a feature of gymnosperms?
A. Presence of naked ovules
B. Formation of fruits
C. Presence of vascular tissues
D. Dominant sporophytic generation
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** The alternation of generations in which the gametophyte and sporophyte are equally dominant or independent is seen in:
A. Algae and Fungi
B. Bryophytes and Pteridophytes
C. Gymnosperms and Angiosperms
D. Only Pteridophytes
**Correct Answer: B**

**29.** Gemmae are asexual reproductive structures found in:
A. Some algae
B. Some gymnosperms
C. Some liverworts
D. Some mosses
**Correct Answer: C**

**30.** Coralloid roots are a feature of *Cycas*. They have a symbiotic association with:
A. Fungi (Mycorrhiza)
B. Nitrogen-fixing cyanobacteria
C. Rhizobium bacteria
D. Algae
**Correct Answer: B**

**31.** In angiosperms, the male gametophyte is the:
A. Stamen
B. Microspore mother cell
C. Pollen grain
D. Nucellus
**Correct Answer: C**

**32.** Which of the following is a living fossil?
A. *Pinus*
B. *Sequoia*
C. *Ginkgo biloba*
D. *Ephedra*
**Correct Answer: C**

**33.** The haplontic life cycle is characteristic of many:
A. Algae like *Volvox* and *Spirogyra*
B. Ferns and mosses
C. Gymnosperms
D. Angiosperms
**Correct Answer: A**

**34.** A plant shows a thallus level of organization. It is haploid and needs water to complete its life cycle because the male gametes are motile. It belongs to:
A. Pteridophytes
B. Gymnosperms
C. Monocots
D. Bryophytes
**Correct Answer: D**

**35.** The unique event in angiosperms, double fertilization, involves:
A. Fusion of two male gametes with the egg
B. Fusion of one male gamete with the egg and the other with the synergids
C. Fusion of one male gamete with the egg and the other with the central cell (polar nuclei)
D. Fusion of two eggs with one male gamete
**Correct Answer: C**

**36.** The plant group that produces spores and embryos but lacks vascular tissues and seeds is:
A. Pteridophyta
B. Rhodophyta
C. Bryophyta
D. Phaeophyta
**Correct Answer: C**

**37.** In pteridophytes, the zygote develops into a young:
A. Gametophyte within the archegonium
B. Sporophyte within the archegonium of the gametophyte
C. Gametophyte on the soil
D. Sporophyte that is independent of the gametophyte
**Correct Answer: B**

**38.** Which of the following is an example of a colonial alga?
A. *Chlamydomonas*
B. *Volvox*
C. *Ulothrix*
D. *Spirogyra*
**Correct Answer: B**

**39.** The pyrenoids in green algal cells are related to:
A. Starch storage
B. Protein storage
C. Both starch and protein storage
D. Fat storage
**Correct Answer: C**

**40.** The sporophylls are aggregated to form compact structures called strobili or cones in:
A. *Marchantia* and *Riccia*
B. *Selaginella* and *Equisetum*
C. *Funaria* and *Sphagnum*
D. All algae
**Correct Answer: B**

#### Hard

**41.** Which of the following statements is correct?
A. Ovules are not enclosed by the ovary wall in gymnosperms.
B. *Selaginella* is homosporous, while *Salvinia* is heterosporous.
C. Stems are usually unbranched in both *Cycas* and *Cedrus*.
D. Horsetails are gymnosperms.
**Correct Answer: A**

**42.** The antherozoids of bryophytes and pteridophytes are flagellated and require water for fertilization. This supports the hypothesis that:
A. They originated in a desert environment.
B. They have an aquatic ancestry.
C. They are more advanced than gymnosperms.
D. They are all homosporous.
**Correct Answer: B**

**43.** The life cycle of an ectocarpus alga is:
A. Haplontic
B. Diplontic
C. Haplo-diplontic
D. Neither haplontic nor diplontic
**Correct Answer: C**

**44.** Read the following five statements (A-E) and select the option with all correct statements:
(A) Mosses and Lichens are the first organisms to colonise a bare rock.
(B) *Selaginella* is a homosporous pteridophyte.
(C) Coralloid roots in *Cycas* have VAM.
(D) Main plant body in bryophytes is gametophytic, whereas in pteridophytes it is sporophytic.
(E) In gymnosperms, male and female gametophytes are present within sporangia located on sporophyte.
A. (A), (D) and (E)
B. (B), (C) and (D)
C. (A), (C) and (D)
D. (B), (C) and (E)
**Correct Answer: A**

**45.** From an evolutionary point of view, which of the following is the most significant feature that led to the dominance of terrestrial plants?
A. The development of flowers
B. The development of the seed habit
C. The development of vascular tissue
D. The development of a dominant gametophyte
**Correct Answer: B**

**46.** If the diploid number of a flowering plant is 36, what would be the chromosome number in its endosperm?
A. 36
B. 18
C. 54
D. 72
**Correct Answer: C**

**47.** In the life cycle of a fern (a pteridophyte), meiosis occurs during the:
A. Formation of spores
B. Formation of gametes
C. Germination of the spore
D. Development of the zygote
**Correct Answer: A**

**48.** A student observed an alga with chlorophyll a, b and phycoerythrin. It also had floridean starch as stored food. The alga belongs to the class:
A. Chlorophyceae
B. Rhodophyceae
C. Phaeophyceae
D. Bacillariophyceae
**Correct Answer: B**

**49.** Consider the life cycle of a typical moss. The correct sequence of events is:
A. Spore → Protonema → Gametophyte → Fertilization → Zygote → Sporophyte → Meiosis
B. Gametophyte → Spore → Protonema → Fertilization → Zygote → Sporophyte → Meiosis
C. Zygote → Sporophyte → Meiosis → Spore → Protonema → Gametophyte → Fertilization
D. Spore → Gametophyte → Fertilization → Zygote → Sporophyte → Meiosis → Protonema
**Correct Answer: A**

**50.** A key difference between the archegonium of a bryophyte and a pteridophyte is that in pteridophytes:
A. The archegonium is a multicellular structure.
B. The neck of the archegonium is shorter.
C. The archegonium is embedded in the gametophyte (prothallus).
D. The archegonium has a venter but no neck.
**Correct Answer: C**

&& Animal Kingdom

#### Easy

**1.** The level of organization in sponges (Phylum Porifera) is:
A. Cellular level
B. Tissue level
C. Organ level
D. Organ system level
**Correct Answer: A**

**2.** The presence of a water transport or canal system is a characteristic feature of the phylum:
A. Coelenterata
B. Porifera
C. Annelida
D. Arthropoda
**Correct Answer: B**

**3.** Cnidoblasts or stinging cells are found in the phylum:
A. Porifera
B. Coelenterata (Cnidaria)
C. Platyhelminthes
D. Annelida
**Correct Answer: B**

**4.** The animals that exhibit radial symmetry are:
A. Annelids
B. Arthropods
C. Molluscs
D. Coelenterates and Echinoderms (adults)
**Correct Answer: D**

**5.** A true coelom (body cavity) is lined by:
A. Ectoderm
B. Endoderm
C. Mesoderm
D. Both ectoderm and endoderm
**Correct Answer: C**

**6.** Flame cells are the excretory structures for:
A. Annelida
B. Platyhelminthes (Flatworms)
C. Aschelminthes (Roundworms)
D. Mollusca
**Correct Answer: B**

**7.** The largest phylum in the animal kingdom is:
A. Mollusca
B. Annelida
C. Chordata
D. Arthropoda
**Correct Answer: D**

**8.** The file-like rasping organ for feeding, called the radula, is present in the phylum:
A. Annelida
B. Arthropoda
C. Mollusca
D. Echinodermata
**Correct Answer: C**

**9.** The presence of a water vascular system is the most distinctive feature of the phylum:
A. Mollusca
B. Echinodermata
C. Hemichordata
D. Chordata
**Correct Answer: B**

**10.** All chordates possess a:
A. Notochord
B. Dorsal hollow nerve cord
C. Pharyngeal gill slits
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**11.** Which of the following is a cold-blooded (poikilothermic) animal?
A. Whale
B. Eagle
C. Snake
D. Human
**Correct Answer: C**

**12.** Birds (Aves) are characterized by the presence of:
A. Scales
B. Feathers
C. Hair
D. A diaphragm
**Correct Answer: B**

**13.** The most unique mammalian characteristic is the presence of:
A. Four-chambered heart
B. Warm blood
C. Mammary glands
D. Lungs
**Correct Answer: C**

**14.** Which of the following is an example of a cartilaginous fish (Chondrichthyes)?
A. Rohu
B. Shark
C. Sea horse
D. Catla
**Correct Answer: B**

**15.** Amphibians respire through:
A. Gills
B. Lungs
C. Skin
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**16.** The body of an arthropod is covered by a chitinous:
A. Endoskeleton
B. Exoskeleton
C. Shell
D. Skin
**Correct Answer: B**

**17.** Metameric segmentation is a characteristic feature of the phylum:
A. Porifera
B. Coelenterata
C. Annelida
D. Mollusca
**Correct Answer: C**

**18.** The excretory organ in insects is the:
A. Green gland
B. Malpighian tubules
C. Nephridia
D. Flame cells
**Correct Answer: B**

**19.** Animals that give birth to young ones are called:
A. Oviparous
B. Viviparous
C. Ovoviviparous
D. Parthenogenetic
**Correct Answer: B**

**20.** A four-chambered heart is present in:
A. Lizards
B. Snakes
C. Frogs
D. Crocodiles
**Correct Answer: D**

#### Medium

**21.** Which of the following is not a characteristic of the phylum Chordata?
A. Presence of a notochord at some stage of life
B. A dorsal hollow nerve cord
C. Pharyngeal gill slits
D. A ventral heart
**Correct Answer: D**
*(Note: The heart is ventral, so this IS a characteristic. The question is often flawed. A better option would be 'Ventral nerve cord'.)*

**22.** Which of the following represents the correct combination without any exception?
A. Class Mammalia - viviparous, hair, four-chambered heart
B. Class Reptilia - scales, three-chambered heart, cold-blooded
C. Class Aves - feathers, beak, warm-blooded, oviparous
D. Class Chondrichthyes - cartilaginous endoskeleton, placoid scales, gill slits without operculum
**Correct Answer: D**

**23.** A pseudocoelom is found in:
A. Platyhelminthes
B. Annelida
C. Arthropoda
D. Aschelminthes (Roundworms)
**Correct Answer: D**

**24.** The phenomenon of alternation of generations (metagenesis) is observed in some:
A. Sponges
B. Cnidarians
C. Ctenophores
D. Annelids
**Correct Answer: B**

**25.** Which of the following is a living fossil?
A. *Pila* (Apple snail)
B. *Limulus* (King crab)
C. *Pinctada* (Pearl oyster)
D. *Octopus*
**Correct Answer: B**

**26.** The air sacs connected to the lungs in birds serve to:
A. Increase body weight
B. Provide a four-chambered heart
C. Supplement respiration and reduce body density
D. Circulate blood
**Correct Answer: C**

**27.** Which of the following animals is not viviparous?
A. Platypus
B. Whale
C. Bat
D. Elephant
**Correct Answer: A**

**28.** The symmetry of an adult echinoderm is:
A. Bilateral
B. Radial
C. Asymmetrical
D. Biradial
**Correct Answer: B**

**29.** The presence of pneumatic bones is a characteristic of:
A. Amphibians
B. Reptiles
C. Aves
D. Mammals
**Correct Answer: C**

**30.** Which of the following is a correct match of a phylum and its excretory organ?
A. Annelida - Flame cells
B. Arthropoda - Nephridia
C. Mollusca - Organs of Bojanus
D. Platyhelminthes - Malpighian tubules
**Correct Answer: C**

**31.** The body cavity of an arthropod is called a:
A. Coelom
B. Pseudocoelom
C. Haemocoel
D. Enterocoel
**Correct Answer: C**

**32.** Which of the following is an exclusive marine phylum?
A. Porifera
B. Coelenterata
C. Echinodermata
D. Mollusca
**Correct Answer: C**

**33.** The transition from aquatic to terrestrial life is first seen in:
A. Fishes
B. Amphibians
C. Reptiles
D. Aves
**Correct Answer: B**

**34.** Which of the following is a correct statement?
A. All chordates are vertebrates.
B. All vertebrates are chordates.
C. All protochordates are invertebrates.
D. All invertebrates are non-chordates.
**Correct Answer: B**

**35.** The presence of an operculum covering the gills is a feature of:
A. Chondrichthyes
B. Osteichthyes
C. Cyclostomata
D. Reptilia
**Correct Answer: B**

**36.** A connecting link between Annelida and Arthropoda is:
A. *Peripatus*
B. *Archaeopteryx*
C. *Limulus*
D. *Balanoglossus*
**Correct Answer: A**

**37.** Bioluminescence is a well-marked feature in the phylum:
A. Coelenterata
B. Ctenophora
C. Platyhelminthes
D. Annelida
**Correct Answer: B**

**38.** Which of the following is an egg-laying mammal?
A. Kangaroo
B. Koala
C. Echidna (Spiny anteater)
D. Bat
**Correct Answer: C**

**39.** The circulatory system in annelids is:
A. Open type
B. Closed type
C. Absent
D. Lacunar type

**40.** The body of which phylum is typically divided into a head, visceral hump, and muscular foot?
A. Annelida
B. Arthropoda
C. Mollusca
D. Echinodermata
**Correct Answer: C**

**41.** Match the following and select the correct option:
Column I          Column II
(a) Choanocytes     (i) Ctenophora
(b) Cnidoblasts     (ii) Platyhelminthes
(c) Flame cells     (iii) Coelenterata
(d) Comb plates     (iv) Porifera
A. a-iv, b-iii, c-ii, d-i
B. a-iii, b-iv, c-i, d-ii
C. a-ii, b-i, c-iv, d-iii
D. a-iv, b-i, c-ii, d-iii

**42.** Which one of the following statements about certain given animals is correct?

C. Molluscs are acoelomates.
D. Insects (Arthropoda) are pseudocoelomates.

A. Jointed appendages
B. Chitinous exoskeleton
C. Metameric segmentation
D. Parapodia
**Correct Answer: D**

**44.** The key difference between Chordates and Non-chordates is:
A. Chordates have a ventral heart, while non-chordates have a dorsal heart (if present).
B. Chordates have a dorsal hollow nerve cord, while non-chordates have a ventral solid nerve cord.
C. Chordates have a post-anal tail, while it is absent in non-chordates.
D. All of the above.
**Correct Answer: D**

**45.** Which of the following represents the correct order of evolution?
A. Fish → Amphibians → Reptiles → Birds → Mammals
B. Amphibians → Fish → Reptiles → Birds → Mammals
C. Fish → Reptiles → Amphibians → Birds → Mammals
D. Fish → Amphibians → Birds → Reptiles → Mammals
**Correct Answer: A**

A. Scorpion
B. Earthworm
C. Snake
D. Starfish
**Correct Answer: C**

(ii) Bilateral symmetry
(iii) True coelomates with segmentation of body
Select the correct option of animal groups which possess all the above characteristics.
A. Annelida, Mollusca and Chordata
B. Annelida, Arthropoda and Chordata
C. Annelida, Arthropoda and Mollusca
D. Arthropoda, Mollusca and Chordata
**Correct Answer: B**

**48.** The larval stage of an echinoderm exhibits:
A. Radial symmetry
B. Bilateral symmetry
C. Asymmetry
D. Spherical symmetry
**Correct Answer: B**

A. Oscula
B. Choanocytes
C. Mesenchymal cells

**50.** Which one of the following is a matching pair of an animal and a certain phenomenon it exhibits?

Alright, let's continue with the Biology chapters. Here are the question sets for the next three chapters, based on the KCET PYQ pattern and with the correct formatting.

***

&& Morphology of Flowering Plants

#### Easy

**1.** The part of the plant that grows towards light is the:
A. Root
B. Stem
C. Leaf
D. Flower
**Correct Answer: B**

**2.** A tap root system develops from the:
A. Radicle
B. Plumule
C. Cotyledon
D. Endosperm
**Correct Answer: A**

**3.** In monocotyledonous plants, the primary root is short-lived and is replaced by a large number of roots. This is known as a:
A. Tap root system
B. Fibrous root system
C. Adventitious root system
D. Prop root system
**Correct Answer: B**

**4.** The arrangement of veins and veinlets in the lamina of a leaf is termed as:
A. Phyllotaxy
B. Venation
C. Aestivation
D. Placentation
**Correct Answer: B**

**5.** A leaf that has a single or undivided lamina is called a:
A. Simple leaf
B. Compound leaf
C. Pinnate leaf
D. Palmate leaf
**Correct Answer: A**

**6.** The arrangement of flowers on the floral axis is termed as:
A. Aestivation
B. Placentation
C. Inflorescence
D. Phyllotaxy
**Correct Answer: C**

**7.** A flower that can be divided into two similar halves by only one particular vertical plane is said to be:
A. Actinomorphic
B. Zygomorphic
C. Asymmetric
D. Isomerous
**Correct Answer: B**

**8.** The arrangement of ovules within the ovary is known as:
A. Aestivation
B. Placentation
C. Venation
D. Cohesion
**Correct Answer: B**

**9.** A fruit that develops from the ovary without fertilization is called a:
A. True fruit
B. False fruit
C. Parthenocarpic fruit
D. Aggregate fruit
**Correct Answer: C**

**10.** A seed with two cotyledons is characteristic of:
A. Monocots
B. Dicots
C. Gymnosperms
D. Pteridophytes
**Correct Answer: B**

**11.** The outermost whorl of a flower, composed of sepals, is the:
A. Calyx
B. Corolla
C. Androecium
D. Gynoecium
**Correct Answer: A**

**12.** Prop roots, as seen in a banyan tree, are a type of:
A. Tap root modification
B. Fibrous root modification
C. Adventitious root modification
D. Stem modification
**Correct Answer: C**

**13.** The pattern of arrangement of leaves on the stem or a branch is called:
A. Venation
B. Inflorescence
C. Aestivation
D. Phyllotaxy
**Correct Answer: D**

**14.** In a hypogynous flower, the ovary is said to be:
A. Superior
B. Inferior
C. Half-inferior
D. Subordinate
**Correct Answer: A**

**15.** The mode of arrangement of sepals or petals in a floral bud is known as:
A. Placentation
B. Aestivation
C. Phyllotaxy
D. Venation
**Correct Answer: B**

**16.** The aleurone layer in a maize grain is rich in:
A. Starch
B. Protein
C. Lipids
D. Vitamins
**Correct Answer: B**

**17.** The edible part of a coconut is the:
A. Endosperm
B. Mesocarp
C. Epicarp
D. Pericarp
**Correct Answer: A**

**18.** The androecium is composed of:
A. Carpels
B. Petals
C. Sepals
D. Stamens
**Correct Answer: D**

**19.** Potato is a modification of the:
A. Root
B. Stem
C. Leaf
D. Fruit
**Correct Answer: B**

**20.** A flower that has all four whorls (calyx, corolla, androecium, gynoecium) is called a:
A. Perfect flower
B. Complete flower
C. Bisexual flower
D. Unisexual flower
**Correct Answer: B**

#### Medium

**21.** The floral formula ⊕ ⚥ K₍₅₎ C₍₅₎ A₅ G₍₂₎ represents the family:
A. Fabaceae
B. Solanaceae
C. Liliaceae
D. Brassicaceae
**Correct Answer: B**

**22.** In a cymose inflorescence, the main axis:
A. Continues to grow indefinitely
B. Terminates in a flower
C. Bears flowers in an acropetal succession
D. Has flowers borne laterally
**Correct Answer: B**

**23.** In marginal placentation, the placenta forms a ridge along the:
A. Central axis of the ovary
B. Ventral suture of the ovary
C. Dorsal suture of the ovary
D. Base of the ovary
**Correct Answer: B**

**24.** Pneumatophores are modifications of roots found in plants growing in:
A. Desert areas
B. Swampy/marshy areas
C. Water
D. Hilly areas
**Correct Answer: B**

**25.** Vexillary aestivation is a characteristic feature of the family:
A. Fabaceae
B. Solanaceae
C. Liliaceae
D. Asteraceae
**Correct Answer: A**

**26.** The technical term used for the androecium in a flower of China rose (*Hibiscus*) is:
A. Monadelphous
B. Diadelphous
C. Polyadelphous
D. Syngenesious
**Correct Answer: A**

**27.** Keel is the characteristic feature of the flower of:
A. Tulip
B. *Indigofera* (Bean)
C. Aloe
D. Tomato
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** When the leaflets are attached at a common point at the tip of the petiole, the leaf is:
A. Pinnately compound
B. Palmately compound
C. Simple
D. Decompound
**Correct Answer: B**

**29.** An example of a plant with parallel venation is:
A. Mango
B. Hibiscus
C. Peepal
D. Maize
**Correct Answer: D**

**30.** The condition where stamens are united into more than two bundles is known as:
A. Monadelphous
B. Diadelphous
C. Polyadelphous
D. Syngenesious
**Correct Answer: C**

**31.** In an epigynous flower like that of a guava, the ovary is:
A. Superior
B. Half-inferior
C. Inferior
D. Absent
**Correct Answer: C**

**32.** A drupe develops from a:
A. Monocarpellary superior ovary and is one-seeded
B. Monocarpellary inferior ovary and is many-seeded
C. Polycarpellary superior ovary and is one-seeded
D. Polycarpellary inferior ovary and is many-seeded
**Correct Answer: A**

**33.** The perianth is the term used when:
A. Calyx and corolla are distinct
B. Calyx and corolla are not distinct
C. Androecium and gynoecium are fused
D. All four whorls are present
**Correct Answer: B**

**34.** Thorns are modifications of the:
A. Stem
B. Leaf
C. Root
D. Stipule
**Correct Answer: A**

**35.** The characteristic inflorescence of the family Solanaceae is:
A. Racemose
B. Spike
C. Solitary axillary or cymose
D. Catkin
**Correct Answer: C**

**36.** An example of a false fruit is:
A. Mango
B. Apple
C. Banana
D. Coconut
**Correct Answer: B**

**37.** The seed coat has two layers, the outer testa and the inner:
A. Tegmen
B. Hilum
C. Micropyle
D. Chalaza
**Correct Answer: A**

**38.** If a single leaf arises at each node, the phyllotaxy is called:
A. Alternate
B. Opposite
C. Whorled
D. Decussate
**Correct Answer: A**

**39.** The tendrils in a pea plant are modifications of the:
A. Stem
B. Axillary bud
C. Leaflet
D. Stipule
**Correct Answer: C**

**40.** A dicotyledonous seed is distinguished from a monocotyledonous seed by the presence of:
A. One cotyledon
B. Two cotyledons
C. An endosperm
D. An aleurone layer
**Correct Answer: B**

**41.** The floral formula K₍₅₎ C₁₊₂₊₍₂₎ A₍₉₎₊₁ G₁ belongs to the family:

B. Mesocarp
C. Endocarp
D. Endosperm
**Correct Answer: B**

**45.** Which of the following is a correct statement?
A. In tomato, the fruit is a capsule.
B. The seeds of orchids have an oil-rich endosperm.
C. The placentation in primrose is free central.
D. The flower of tulip is a zygomorphic flower.
**Correct Answer: C**

**46.** The 'eye' of the potato tuber represents the:
A. Root cap
B. Axillary bud
C. Apical bud
D. Flower bud
**Correct Answer: B**

**47.** In a China rose flower, the aestivation of the petals is:
A. Valvate
B. Twisted
C. Imbricate
D. Vexillary
**Correct Answer: B**

**48.** A fibrous root system is better adapted than a tap root system for:
A. Storage of food
B. Anchorage of the plant in the soil
C. Absorption of water and minerals from the surface soil
D. Conduction of water to aerial parts
**Correct Answer: C**

**49.** In Australian Acacia, the petiole expands and becomes green to perform the function of photosynthesis. This modified structure is called a:
A. Phylloclade
B. Cladode
C. Phyllode
D. Pitcher
**Correct Answer: C**

**50.** The scutellum observed in a grain of wheat or maize is comparable to which part of the seed in other monocotyledons?
A. Cotyledon
B. Endosperm
C. Aleurone layer
D. Plumule
**Correct Answer: A**

***

&& Anatomy of Flowering Plants

#### Easy

**1.** A group of cells having a common origin and usually performing a common function is called a:
A. Tissue
B. Organ
C. Organ system
D. Cell
**Correct Answer: A**

**2.** The tissue responsible for the growth in length of a plant is the:
A. Lateral meristem
B. Apical meristem
C. Intercalary meristem
D. Permanent tissue
**Correct Answer: B**

**3.** Which of the following is a simple permanent tissue?
A. Xylem
B. Phloem
C. Parenchyma
D. Epidermis
**Correct Answer: C**

**4.** The complex tissue responsible for the conduction of water and minerals is:
A. Phloem
B. Xylem
C. Sclerenchyma
D. Collenchyma
**Correct Answer: B**

**5.** The main function of collenchyma tissue is:
A. Photosynthesis
B. Storage
C. Mechanical support to growing parts
D. Conduction of water
**Correct Answer: C**

**6.** The outermost layer of the plant body is the:
A. Cortex
B. Endodermis
C. Epidermis
D. Pericycle
**Correct Answer: A**

**7.** Stomata are structures found in the epidermis of:
A. Roots
B. Stems
C. Leaves
D. Flowers
**Correct Answer: C**

**8.** The vascular bundles in a dicot stem are arranged in a:
A. Scattered manner
B. Ring
C. Radial pattern
D. Concentric pattern
**Correct Answer: B**

**9.** Secondary growth in a dicot stem is brought about by the activity of the:
A. Apical meristem
B. Intercalary meristem
C. Vascular cambium and cork cambium
D. Pericycle
**Correct Answer: C**

**10.** Phloem tissue is primarily responsible for the transport of:
A. Water
B. Minerals
C. Food (sugars)
D. Air
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** Sclerenchyma cells are characterized by their:
A. Thin walls and large vacuoles
B. Thickened corners with pectin
C. Thick, lignified walls and are often dead
D. Ability to divide continuously
**Correct Answer: C**

**12.** The vascular bundles which have cambium between the xylem and phloem are called:
A. Closed
B. Open
C. Radial
D. Conjoint
**Correct Answer: B**

**13.** The central-most region of a dicot stem is the:
A. Cortex
B. Pith (or Medulla)
C. Pericycle
D. Endodermis
**Correct Answer: B**

**14.** In a dicot leaf, the vascular bundles are surrounded by a layer of thick-walled cells called the:
A. Epidermis
B. Mesophyll
C. Bundle sheath
D. Cuticle
**Correct Answer: C**

**15.** The dead, central, dark-coloured, and hard part of a secondary xylem is called:
A. Sapwood
B. Heartwood
C. Bark
D. Cork
**Correct Answer: B**

**16.** Which of the following is not a part of the phloem?
A. Sieve tubes
B. Companion cells
C. Phloem parenchyma
D. Tracheids
**Correct Answer: D**

**17.** The tissue system that forms the main bulk of the plant body is the:
A. Epidermal tissue system
B. Vascular tissue system
C. Ground tissue system
D. Meristematic tissue system
**Correct Answer: C**

**18.** The growth of roots and stems in length with the help of apical meristems is called:
A. Primary growth
B. Secondary growth
C. Lateral growth
D. Intercalary growth
**Correct Answer: A**

**19.** The bark of a tree includes:
A. Only the cork
B. Only the secondary phloem
C. All tissues external to the vascular cambium
D. Only the periderm
**Correct Answer: C**

**20.** The stomata in a dicot leaf are more numerous on the:
A. Upper epidermis (adaxial)
B. Lower epidermis (abaxial)
C. They are equally distributed
D. They are absent
**Correct Answer: B**

---

#### Medium

**21.** The vascular bundles in a monocot stem are:
A. Conjoint, open, and arranged in a ring
B. Radial, open, and scattered
C. Conjoint, closed, and scattered
D. Radial, closed, and arranged in a ring
**Correct Answer: C**

**22.** The casparian strips are a characteristic feature of the:
A. Epidermis
B. Cortex
C. Endodermis
D. Pericycle
**Correct Answer: C**

**23.** A monocot leaf is distinguished from a dicot leaf by the presence of:
A. Stomata on both surfaces (isobilateral)
B. Differentiated palisade and spongy mesophyll
C. Reticulate venation
D. Bulliform cells in some cases
**Correct Answer: A**
*(Note: Bulliform cells are also a key feature in many monocots)*

**24.** The vascular cambium in a dicot root is:
A. Entirely primary in origin
B. Entirely secondary in origin
C. Partially primary and partially secondary in origin
D. Absent
**Correct Answer: B**

**25.** The main function of the lenticels is:
A. Photosynthesis
B. Transpiration
C. Gaseous exchange
D. Food storage
**Correct Answer: C**

**26.** In a dicot root, the vascular bundles are radial and the number of xylem arms is usually:
A. One (monarch)
B. Two (diarch)
C. Four (tetrarch)
D. Many (polyarch)
**Correct Answer: C**

**27.** The age of a tree can be estimated by:
A. Its height and girth
B. The thickness of its bark
C. The number of annual rings
D. The biomass
**Correct Answer: C**

**28.** The companion cells are closely associated with the:
A. Tracheids
B. Vessels
C. Sieve tubes
D. Sclereids
**Correct Answer: C**

**29.** The ground tissue in a dicot leaf, called mesophyll, is differentiated into:
A. Palisade and spongy parenchyma
B. Xylem and phloem parenchyma
C. Upper and lower epidermis
D. Collenchyma and sclerenchyma
**Correct Answer: A**

**30.** Which of the following is absent in the phloem of most monocots?
A. Sieve tubes
B. Companion cells
C. Phloem parenchyma
D. Phloem fibres
**Correct Answer: C**

**31.** The lateral roots in a dicot plant originate from the:
A. Endodermis
B. Cortex
C. Epidermis
D. Pericycle
**Correct Answer: D**

**32.** In a conjoint and collateral vascular bundle:
A. Xylem and phloem are on different radii
B. Xylem and phloem are on the same radius with xylem on the outer side
C. Xylem and phloem are on the same radius with phloem on the outer side
D. Xylem surrounds the phloem
**Correct Answer: C**

**33.** Heartwood is different from sapwood in that it:
A. Conducts water and minerals efficiently
B. Is light in colour and susceptible to pests
C. Is a dead, central, and mechanically strong part
D. Is the outer region of the secondary xylem
**Correct Answer: C**

**34.** Which of the following is living and provides mechanical strength?
A. Parenchyma
B. Collenchyma
C. Sclerenchyma fibres
D. Sclereids
**Correct Answer: B**

**35.** The meristem that occurs between mature tissues is known as:
A. Apical meristem
B. Lateral meristem
C. Intercalary meristem
D. Phellogen
**Correct Answer: C**

**36.** A bicollateral vascular bundle is characterized by:
A. Phloem on both outer and inner sides of the xylem
B. Xylem on both outer and inner sides of the phloem
C. Phloem and xylem on different radii
D. Phloem and xylem scattered in the ground tissue
**Correct Answer: A**

**37.** Bulliform cells are found in the leaves of certain grasses and they help in:
A. Photosynthesis
B. Gaseous exchange
C. Minimizing water loss by rolling the leaves
D. Storing food
**Correct Answer: C**

**38.** The cork cambium, cork, and secondary cortex are collectively called:
A. Phelloderm
B. Phellogen
C. Periderm
D. Phellem
**Correct Answer: C**

**39.** The only living component of the xylem tissue is:
A. Tracheids
B. Vessels
C. Xylem fibres
D. Xylem parenchyma
**Correct Answer: D**

**40.** A dicot stem is identified by the presence of:
A. Scattered vascular bundles
B. Vascular bundles arranged in a ring
C. Radial vascular bundles
D. Absence of pith
**Correct Answer: B**

---

#### Hard

**41.** Water-containing cavities in vascular bundles are found in:
A. Dicot stems
B. Monocot stems
C. Dicot roots
D. Monocot roots
**Correct Answer: B**

**42.** The vascular cambium of a dicot stem is:
A. A single layer of cells
B. A multi-layered structure
C. Composed of dead cells
D. Formed from the pericycle only
**Correct Answer: A**

**43.** When the phellogen (cork cambium) cuts off cells towards the inner side, it differentiates into the:
A. Cork (phellem)
B. Secondary cortex (phelloderm)
C. Secondary xylem
D. Secondary phloem
**Correct Answer: B**

**44.** In a dorsiventral (dicot) leaf, the protoxylem is situated towards the:
A. Adaxial (upper) surface
B. Abaxial (lower) surface
C. Centre of the vascular bundle
D. Phloem
**Correct Answer: A**

**45.** A tree has 10 annual rings, its cambium is 5 years old. The total age of the tree is:
A. 5 years
B. 10 years
C. 15 years
D. Cannot be determined
**Correct Answer: B**
*(Note: Cambium age is irrelevant to the total age shown by rings)*

**46.** A conjoint, collateral, and open vascular bundle is a characteristic of:
A. Monocot stem
B. Dicot stem
C. Monocot root
D. Dicot root
**Correct Answer: B**

**47.** Sieve tubes are better suited for translocation because they:
A. Are much broader than other cells
B. Possess a bordered pit
C. Possess no end walls
D. Possess a perforated cross wall and have no nucleus at maturity
**Correct Answer: D**

**48.** The transition from radial to conjoint vascular bundles occurs in which part of the plant?
A. In the stem apex
B. In the root apex
C. In the hypocotyl region (stem-root transition zone)
D. In the leaves
**Correct Answer: C**

**49.** Passage cells are thin-walled cells found in the:
A. Epidermis of roots to allow water entry
B. Pericycle of roots to form lateral roots
C. Endodermis of roots to facilitate water movement to the xylem
D. Pith of stems for storage
**Correct Answer: C**

**50.** The springwood (or early wood) differs from autumn wood (or late wood) in that it:
A. Has wider vessels and is lighter in colour
B. Has narrower vessels and is darker in colour
C. Is formed during the winter season
D. Has a higher density
**Correct Answer: A**

***

&& Structural Organisation in Animals

#### Easy

**1.** A group of similar cells along with intercellular substances that perform a specific function is known as a:
A. Organ
B. Organ system
C. Tissue
D. Organism
**Correct Answer: C**

**2.** The tissue that covers the outside of the body and lines the organs and cavities is:
A. Connective tissue
B. Muscular tissue
C. Epithelial tissue
D. Neural tissue
**Correct Answer: C**

**3.** Which of the following is not a type of connective tissue?
A. Blood
B. Bone
C. Cartilage
D. Muscle
**Correct Answer: D**

**4. The muscle tissue that is voluntary and striated is:**
A. Skeletal muscle
B. Smooth muscle
C. Cardiac muscle
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: A**

**5.** The basic unit of the neural system is the:
A. Nephron
B. Neuron
C. Osteocyte
D. Chondrocyte
**Correct Answer: B**

**6.** The circulatory system of an earthworm is of the:
A. Open type
B. Closed type
C. Lacunar type
D. Absent
**Correct Answer: B**

**7.** The body of a cockroach is covered by a hard exoskeleton made of:
A. Chitin
B. Cellulose
C. Pectin
D. Calcium carbonate
**Correct Answer: A**

**8.** The excretory organs in an earthworm are:
A. Malpighian tubules
B. Flame cells
C. Nephridia
D. Kidneys
**Correct Answer: C**

**9.** The heart of a cockroach has how many chambers?
A. 2
B. 4
C. 10
D. 13
**Correct Answer: D**

**10.** A frog is a(n):
A. Reptile
B. Mammal
C. Amphibian
D. Fish
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** Tendons connect:
A. Bone to bone
B. Muscle to bone
C. Muscle to muscle
D. Nerve to muscle
**Correct Answer: B**

**12.** The simple epithelium consisting of a single layer of flattened cells is called:
A. Cuboidal epithelium
B. Columnar epithelium
C. Squamous epithelium
D. Ciliated epithelium
**Correct Answer: C**

**13.** Blood is considered a type of connective tissue because:
A. It connects different parts of the body
B. It is formed from mesoderm and has a fluid matrix
C. It transports oxygen
D. It contains haemoglobin
**Correct Answer: B**

**14.** The segments of an earthworm are called:
A. Proglottids
B. Strobila
C. Metameres
D. Ostia
**Correct Answer: C**

**15.** The respiratory pigment in the blood of a frog is:
A. Haemocyanin
B. Haemoglobin dissolved in plasma
C. Haemoglobin in RBCs
D. Absent
**Correct Answer: C**

**16.** The cells of cartilage tissue are called:
A. Osteocytes
B. Chondrocytes
C. Fibroblasts
D. Mast cells
**Correct Answer: B**

**17.** Smooth muscles are found in the:
A. Walls of the heart
B. Biceps of the arm
C. Walls of internal organs like the intestine
D. Thigh muscles
**Correct Answer: C**

**18.** The body of a cockroach is divisible into:
A. Head and trunk
B. Head, thorax, and abdomen
C. Cephalothorax and abdomen
D. Head, neck, and trunk
**Correct Answer: B**

**19.** Earthworms are hermaphrodites, which means:
A. They can live on both land and water
B. They are unisexual
C. Both testes and ovaries are present in the same individual
D. They reproduce asexually
**Correct Answer: C**

**20.** The skin of a frog is:
A. Dry and scaly
B. Covered with feathers
C. Moist and smooth
D. Covered with hair
**Correct Answer: C**

---

#### Medium

**21.** The type of epithelium found in the lining of the kidney tubules and ducts of glands is:
A. Simple squamous
B. Simple cuboidal
C. Simple columnar
D. Ciliated
**Correct Answer: B**

**22.** Which of the following tissues provides a supporting framework for the epithelium?
A. Areolar connective tissue
B. Adipose tissue
C. Dense regular tissue
D. Bone
**Correct Answer: A**

**23.** Intercalated discs are characteristic features of:
A. Skeletal muscles
B. Smooth muscles
C. Cardiac muscles
D. Neural tissue
**Correct Answer: C**

**24.** The clitellum in an earthworm is a prominent dark band of glandular tissue present in which segments?
A. 5-7
B. 9-11
C. 14-16
D. 20-22
**Correct Answer: C**

**25.** The respiratory system of a cockroach consists of a network of tubes called:
A. Bronchi
B. Alveoli
C. Trachea
D. Gills
**Correct Answer: C**

**26.** The heart of a frog has:
A. Two atria and one ventricle
B. One atrium and two ventricles
C. Two atria and two ventricles
D. One atrium and one ventricle
**Correct Answer: A**

**27.** Ligaments are made of:
A. White fibrous connective tissue
B. Yellow elastic connective tissue
C. Areolar tissue
D. Adipose tissue
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** The function of Malpighian tubules in a cockroach is:
A. Respiration
B. Digestion
C. Reproduction
D. Excretion
**Correct Answer: D**

**29.** The typhlosole in an earthworm is a fold of the intestinal wall that:
A. Secretes digestive enzymes
B. Increases the surface area for absorption
C. Grinds food particles
D. Stores food
**Correct Answer: B**

**30.** A frog undergoes hibernation during winter. This is called:
A. Aestivation
B. Hibernation
C. Metamorphosis
D. Paedogenesis
**Correct Answer: B**

**31.** The blood of an earthworm is red due to the presence of:
A. Haemoglobin in RBCs
B. Haemoglobin dissolved in plasma
C. Haemocyanin in plasma
D. Myoglobin in muscles
**Correct Answer: B**

**32.** The mosaic vision in a cockroach is formed with the help of multiple simple eyes called:
A. Ocelli
B. Ommatidia
C. Fenestrae
D. Setae
**Correct Answer: B**

**33.** The type of cell junctions that help to stop substances from leaking across a tissue are called:
A. Adhering junctions
B. Gap junctions
C. Tight junctions
D. Desmosomes
**Correct Answer: C**

**34.** Which of the following is a product of the salivary glands of a cockroach?
A. Amylase
B. Trypsin
C. Lipase
D. Pepsin
**Correct Answer: A**

**35.** The central nervous system of an earthworm consists of a nerve ring and a:
A. Dorsal, solid, and single nerve cord
B. Ventral, solid, and double nerve cord
C. Dorsal, hollow, and single nerve cord
D. Ventral, hollow, and double nerve cord
**Correct Answer: B**

**36.** The specialized connective tissue consisting of a solid and pliable matrix that resists compression is:
A. Bone
B. Cartilage
C. Adipose tissue
D. Blood
**Correct Answer: B**

**37.** The brain of a frog is enclosed in a bony box called the:
A. Cranium
B. Vertebral column
C. Sternum
D. Pelvic girdle
**Correct Answer: A**

**38.** The compound epithelial tissue:
A. Has a limited role in secretion and absorption
B. Consists of a single layer of cells
C. Is mainly found lining blood vessels
D. Allows diffusion across it
**Correct Answer: A**

**39.** The anal cerci are paired, jointed structures found in cockroaches that are present on the:
A. 7th abdominal segment in males
B. 9th abdominal segment in females
C. 10th abdominal segment in both sexes
D. 10th abdominal segment in males only
**Correct Answer: C**

**40.** A frog's vertebra is of the type:
A. Acoelous
B. Amphicoelous
C. Procoelous
D. Heterocoelous
**Correct Answer: C**

#### Hard

**41.** The correct sequence of parts in the alimentary canal of a cockroach is:
A. Pharynx → Oesophagus → Crop → Gizzard → Ileum → Colon → Rectum
B. Pharynx → Oesophagus → Gizzard → Crop → Ileum → Colon → Rectum
C. Oesophagus → Pharynx → Crop → Gizzard → Ileum → Rectum → Colon
D. Oesophagus → Crop → Pharynx → Gizzard → Ileum → Colon → Rectum
**Correct Answer: A**

**42.** The Haversian canal system is a characteristic feature of:
A. Avian bone
B. Reptilian bone
C. Mammalian bone
D. Cartilage
**Correct Answer: C**

**43.** The spermathecae in an earthworm:
A. Produce sperm
B. Store sperm received from another worm during copulation
C. Produce eggs
D. Are involved in nourishing the sperm
**Correct Answer: B**

**44.** In which of the following tissues are the cells held together with little intercellular material?
A. Connective tissue
B. Muscular tissue
C. Epithelial tissue
D. Neural tissue
**Correct Answer: C**

**45.** The function of the Bidder's canal in a male frog is to:
A. Carry urine from the kidney
B. Carry sperm from the testes to the kidney
C. Carry eggs from the ovary
D. Filter blood
**Correct Answer: B**

**46.** Which of the following is not a secretion of the exocrine glands?
A. Saliva
B. Mucus
C. Earwax
D. Hormones
**Correct Answer: D**

**47.** The forestomach of a cockroach consists of:
A. Crop and gizzard
B. Gizzard and hepatic caeca
C. Crop and hepatic caeca
D. Mesenteron and hindgut
**Correct Answer: A**

**48.** The type of epithelium that provides protection against chemical and mechanical stresses is:
A. Simple squamous epithelium
B. Simple cuboidal epithelium
C. Simple columnar epithelium
D. Compound epithelium
**Correct Answer: D**

**49.** A key difference between the circulatory system of an earthworm and a cockroach is:
A. The presence of a heart
B. The presence of blood vessels
C. The presence of a coloured respiratory pigment
D. The direction of blood flow
**Correct Answer: C**

**50.** The inner lining of the gut, known as the peritrophic membrane, is absent in which part of the cockroach's alimentary canal?
A. Foregut
B. Midgut
C. Hindgut
D. Both A and C
**Correct Answer: D**

***

&& Cell-The Unit of Life

#### Easy

**1.** Which of the following is known as the 'powerhouse' of the cell?
A. Nucleus
B. Ribosome
C. Mitochondrion
D. Lysosome
**Correct Answer: C**

**2.** The cell theory was proposed by:
A. Watson and Crick
B. Schleiden and Schwann
C. Robert Hooke
D. Antonie van Leeuwenhoek
**Correct Answer: B**

**3.** A cell without a well-defined nucleus and membrane-bound organelles is a:
A. Eukaryotic cell
B. Prokaryotic cell
C. Plant cell
D. Animal cell
**Correct Answer: B**

**4.** The suicidal bags of the cell are the:
A. Ribosomes
B. Lysosomes
C. Golgi apparatus
D. Mitochondria
**Correct Answer: B**

**5.** The cell wall of a plant cell is mainly composed of:
A. Chitin
B. Peptidoglycan
C. Cellulose
D. Lignin
**Correct Answer: C**

**6.** Which organelle is responsible for protein synthesis?
A. Mitochondrion
B. Lysosome
C. Ribosome
D. Vacuole
**Correct Answer: C**

**7.** The fluid mosaic model of the plasma membrane was proposed by:
A. Schleiden and Schwann
B. Singer and Nicolson
C. Robert Brown
D. Camillo Golgi
**Correct Answer: B**

**8.** The outermost layer of a bacterial cell envelope is the:
A. Plasma membrane
B. Cell wall
C. Glycocalyx
D. Cytoplasm
**Correct Answer: C**

**9.** The control center of a eukaryotic cell is the:
A. Nucleolus
B. Cytoplasm
C. Nucleus
D. Ribosome
**Correct Answer: C**

**10.** Plastids that contain chlorophyll and are involved in photosynthesis are called:
A. Chromoplasts
B. Leucoplasts
C. Chloroplasts
D. Amyloplasts
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** The 70S type of ribosome is found in:
A. Eukaryotic cytoplasm
B. Prokaryotic cells and mitochondria
C. Nucleus
D. Golgi apparatus
**Correct Answer: B**

**12.** The site of aerobic respiration in a eukaryotic cell is the:
A. Ribosome
B. Cytoplasm
C. Mitochondrion
D. Chloroplast
**Correct Answer: C**

**13.** The single membrane that bounds a vacuole is called the:
A. Plasmalemma
B. Tonoplast
C. Cell wall
D. Nuclear membrane
**Correct Answer: B**

**14.** In a eukaryotic cell, the endoplasmic reticulum is involved in:
A. Protein synthesis and lipid synthesis
B. Photosynthesis
C. Respiration
D. DNA replication
**Correct Answer: A**

**15.** The Golgi apparatus is primarily involved in:
A. Protein synthesis
B. Cellular respiration
C. Packaging and modification of materials
D. Fat digestion
**Correct Answer: C**

**16.** The cell organelle that is absent in animal cells but present in plant cells is the:
A. Nucleus
B. Mitochondrion
C. Ribosome
D. Plastid
**Correct Answer: D**

**17.** The cytoskeleton in a cell is involved in:
A. Mechanical support and motility
B. Protein synthesis
C. Energy production
D. Storage
**Correct Answer: A**

**18.** The 'Omnis cellula-e cellula' (all cells arise from pre-existing cells) concept was given by:
A. Schleiden
B. Schwann
C. Rudolf Virchow
D. Robert Hooke
**Correct Answer: C**

**19.** Mesosomes in prokaryotes are infoldings of the cell membrane that help in:
A. DNA replication and respiration
B. Protein synthesis
C. Photosynthesis
D. Motility
**Correct Answer: A**

**20.** Cilia and flagella are locomotory structures made of:
A. Actin filaments
B. Myosin filaments
C. Keratin
D. Microtubules
**Correct Answer: D**

---

#### Medium

**21.** The correct sequence of layers in a bacterial cell envelope from outside to inside is:
A. Cell wall → Glycocalyx → Plasma membrane
B. Glycocalyx → Cell wall → Plasma membrane
C. Plasma membrane → Cell wall → Glycocalyx
D. Glycocalyx → Plasma membrane → Cell wall
**Correct Answer: B**

**22.** Which of the following is not a part of the endomembrane system?
A. Golgi complex
B. Endoplasmic Reticulum
C. Mitochondria
D. Lysosomes
**Correct Answer: C**

**23.** The ribosomes of a polysome translate the mRNA into:
A. DNA
B. Lipids
C. Carbohydrates
D. Proteins
**Correct Answer: D**

**24.** The cis and trans faces of the Golgi apparatus are:
A. Similar in structure and function
B. The forming face and the maturing face, respectively
C. The maturing face and the forming face, respectively
D. Both involved in protein synthesis
**Correct Answer: B**

**25.** The cristae in mitochondria are infoldings of the inner membrane that:
A. Increase the surface area for ATP synthesis
B. Store proteins
C. Are the site of glycolysis
D. Contain the genetic material
**Correct Answer: A**

**26.** The stroma of the chloroplast contains:
A. Light-harvesting pigments
B. Enzymes for the light-dependent reactions
C. Enzymes for the Calvin cycle (carbon fixation)
D. The electron transport chain
**Correct Answer: C**

**27.** The arrangement of microtubules in a eukaryotic cilium or flagellum is:
A. 9 + 0
B. 9 + 2
C. 9 + 1
D. 9 + 3
**Correct Answer: B**

**28.** The function of the centrosome and centrioles in an animal cell is:
A. To form the basal body of cilia and flagella
B. To form the spindle fibres during cell division
C. To organize the microtubules
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

**29.** The main arena of various cellular activities in both plant and animal cells is the:
A. Nucleus
B. Cytoplasm
C. Mitochondrion
D. Cell membrane
**Correct Answer: B**

**30.** A cell that is very active in the synthesis and secretion of proteins would be expected to have a large number of:
A. Lysosomes
B. Ribosomes
C. Smooth ER
D. Mitochondria
**Correct Answer: B**

**31.** The middle lamella of the plant cell wall is mainly composed of:
A. Cellulose
B. Pectin
C. Lignin
D. Suberin
**Correct Answer: B**

**32.** According to the fluid mosaic model, the plasma membrane is composed of:
A. A phospholipid bilayer with embedded proteins
B. A protein bilayer with embedded phospholipids
C. A solid layer of proteins and lipids
D. A carbohydrate layer with embedded proteins
**Correct Answer: A**

**33.** Which of the following is a function of the smooth endoplasmic reticulum?
A. Synthesis of proteins
B. Synthesis of lipids and steroids
C. Formation of lysosomes
D. Breakdown of foreign material
**Correct Answer: B**

**34.** A chromosome with a centromere slightly away from the middle, resulting in one shorter arm and one longer arm, is called:
A. Metacentric
B. Sub-metacentric
C. Acrocentric
D. Telocentric
**Correct Answer: B**

**35.** The nucleus contains a dense, spherical structure that is the site of ribosomal RNA synthesis. This structure is the:
A. Chromatin
B. Nuclear pore
C. Nucleolus
D. Karyolymph
**Correct Answer: C**

**36.** The movement of water across the plasma membrane from a region of high concentration to low concentration is called:
A. Active transport
B. Diffusion
C. Osmosis
D. Facilitated diffusion
**Correct Answer: C**

**37.** The stacks of flattened, disc-shaped sacs in a chloroplast are known as:
A. Stroma
B. Grana
C. Thylakoids
D. Frets
**Correct Answer: B**

**38.** Which of the following statements about prokaryotic cells is incorrect?
A. They lack a nuclear membrane.
B. Their genetic material is naked.
C. They contain membrane-bound organelles.
D. They have 70S ribosomes.
**Correct Answer: C**

**39.** The two subunits of the 80S ribosome are:
A. 50S and 30S
B. 60S and 40S
C. 40S and 40S
D. 50S and 40S
**Correct Answer: B**

**40.** The nuclear envelope is a two-membrane structure that is interrupted by minute pores. These pores are formed by:
A. The fusion of the two membranes
B. The action of lysosomes
C. The presence of ribosomes
D. The extension of the ER
**Correct Answer: A**

C. Solubility
D. Shape

A. Metacentric

D. Telocentric
**Correct Answer: C**

**45.** A major site for the synthesis of lipids is the:
A. Rough ER
B. Smooth ER
C. Nucleoplasm
D. Symplast
**Correct Answer: B**

**46.** The plasma membrane helps in:
A. Transportation of molecules across it
B. Cell growth and division
C. Formation of intercellular junctions
D. All of the above
**Correct Answer: D**

D. Lysosomes

A. Starch
B. Proteins
C. Fats and oils
D. Chlorophyll

**49.** The core of a cilium or flagellum, called the axoneme, possesses a number of microtubules running parallel to the long axis. The arrangement of these microtubules is:
A. A ring of nine doublets and a pair of centrally located microtubules (9+2)
B. A ring of nine singlets and two central singlets (9+2)
C. Nine triplets arranged in a circle (9+0)
D. Nine doublets arranged in a circle (9+0)

**50.** The non-membranous organelle, the centriole, is found in:
A. All eukaryotic cells

&& Biomolecules

#### Easy

**1.** The most abundant chemical in living organisms is:
A. Protein
B. Water
C. Carbohydrate
D. Nucleic acid
**Correct Answer: B**

**2.** The building blocks of proteins are:
A. Fatty acids
B. Glucose units
C. Amino acids
D. Nucleotides
**Correct Answer: C**

**3.** Which of the following is a polysaccharide?
A. Glucose
B. Fructose
C. Sucrose
D. Starch
**Correct Answer: D**

**4.** A peptide bond is formed between two:
A. Monosaccharides
B. Fatty acids
C. Amino acids
D. Nucleotides
**Correct Answer: C**

**5.** The primary structure of a protein refers to its:
A. Three-dimensional shape
B. Helical structure
C. Sequence of amino acids
D. Subunit arrangement
**Correct Answer: C**

**6.** DNA and RNA are types of:
A. Proteins
B. Lipids
C. Carbohydrates
D. Nucleic acids
**Correct Answer: D**

**7.** Enzymes are biological catalysts that are chemically:
A. Proteins
B. Carbohydrates
C. Lipids
D. Vitamins
**Correct Answer: A**

**8.** The sugar found in DNA is:
A. Ribose
B. Deoxyribose
C. Glucose
D. Fructose
**Correct Answer: B**

**9.** Which of the following is not a component of a nucleotide?
A. A phosphate group
B. A nitrogenous base
C. A pentose sugar
D. A fatty acid
**Correct Answer: D**

**10.** Lipids are generally insoluble in water but soluble in:
A. Acids
B. Bases
C. Organic solvents
D. Saline solutions
**Correct Answer: C**

**11.** The alpha-helix and beta-pleated sheet are examples of a protein's:
A. Primary structure
B. Secondary structure
C. Tertiary structure
D. Quaternary structure
**Correct Answer: B**

**12.** The nitrogenous base that is present in RNA but absent in DNA is:
A. Adenine
B. Guanine
C. Cytosine
D. Uracil
**Correct Answer: D**

**13.** The place on an enzyme where the substrate binds is called the:
A. Active site
B. Allosteric site
C. Catalytic site
D. Regulatory site
**Correct Answer: A**

**14.** Glycogen is a storage polysaccharide found in:
A. Plants
B. Animals
C. Fungi
D. Bacteria
**Correct Answer: B**

**15.** Which of the following is an essential amino acid?
A. Alanine
B. Glycine
C. Proline
D. Leucine
**Correct Answer: D**

**16.** The model of an enzyme's action where the active site changes shape to fit the substrate is called the:
A. Lock and key model
B. Induced fit model
C. Fluid mosaic model
D. Template model
**Correct Answer: B**

**17.** The process of an enzyme losing its three-dimensional structure and catalytic activity due to heat or pH changes is called:
A. Denaturation
B. Renaturation
C. Hydrolysis
D. Saturation
**Correct Answer: A**

**18.** The two strands of a DNA molecule are held together by:
A. Covalent bonds
B. Ionic bonds
C. Peptide bonds
D. Hydrogen bonds
**Correct Answer: D**

**19.** A non-protein organic molecule that is necessary for the proper functioning of an enzyme is called a:
A. Co-factor
B. Co-enzyme
C. Apoenzyme
D. Holoenzyme
**Correct Answer: B**

**20.** Which of the following is a saturated fatty acid?
A. Oleic acid
B. Linoleic acid
C. Palmitic acid
D. Arachidonic acid
**Correct Answer: C**

A. Primary structure

**35.** The reaction rate of an enzyme-catalyzed reaction doubles for every:
A. 1°C rise in temperature

**36.** A phosphodiester bond is present in:

**39.** The Michaelis-Menten constant (Km) is the substrate concentration at which the reaction velocity is:
A. Maximum (Vmax)
B. Half of the maximum (Vmax/2)

**40.** The bond between the phosphate and the hydroxyl group of a sugar in a nucleic acid is a(n):
